Otherwise `reachable`. UI: a per-row "Test" Button in the ConnectorRegistry tile, status surfaced via the existing `StatusDot` (ok/bad/pending) + a label, per-row status map (mirrors old McpServerForm). | The card is explicit "Optional polish" and says a lighter CLI/packages check is fine. A REAL outbound MCP connect (what the old `/test` did) would need a brand-new host-side reachability hook + sandbox/network egress + untrusted-remote-response handling ‚Äî a far larger security surface for an optional affordance, and the connectors plugin can't import mcp-client's connection layer (invariant #2). Credential-presence + config-sanity needs ZERO new network egress, works uniformly across MCP and CLI/packages connectors, and maps cleanly onto the three required states. `credentials:list` is already a metadata-only read (no secret leak). | (a) real MCP connect+listTools probe via a new `connectors:probe`/`mcp:test` host hook ‚Üí DEFERRED as a follow-up (heavier, security-reviewed network surface; the card calls it optional). (b) client-only heuristic (no server round-trip) ‚Üí REJECTED: the client never sees `capabilities` for the list summary AND can't read the vault, so credential presence isn't client-derivable. |

## 2026-06-01 ‚Äî TASK-107 per-agent connector-attachment store (replace mcpConfigIds stopgap)

| Date | Decision | Rationale | Alternatives |
|---|---|---|---|
| 2026-06-01 | **The per-agent connector-attachment store is a new `connector_attachments JSONB NOT NULL DEFAULT '[]'` column on `agents_v1_agents`, holding a plain `string[]` of connector ids ‚Äî mirroring `skill_attachments` EXACTLY.** New `agents:set-connector-attachments` hook (actor+agentId+connectorIds ‚Üí {agent}), `connectorAttachments` surfaced on the `Agent` DTO + `agents:resolve` output + serializeAgent + a `PATCH /admin/agents/:id/connector-attachments` route. | Invariant #4: the agent is the unit of attachment; @ax/agents owns agent config. A connector attachment needs NO credentialBindings (unlike SkillAttachment) ‚Äî the connector owns its own slots and the cred ref derives from keyMode‚Üíscope (TASK-96), so `string[]` is the right shape. Mirrors the proven skill_attachments column+hook+route precedent ‚Üí low blast radius. | (a) a separate `agents_v1_connector_attachments` side-table ‚Äî REJECTED, skill_attachments set the JSONB-column precedent + a tiny id list doesn't warrant a join table. (b) keep it in @ax/connectors keyed by agent_id ‚Äî REJECTED, would split the agent's config across two plugins (the agent-global attachment is admin-managed agent config, exactly like skill_attachments which lives in @ax/agents per the 2026-05-26 TASK-33 decision). |
| 2026-06-01 | **Connector attachments do NOT participate in the wildcard sentinel; `mcpConfigIds` reverts to MCP-only meaning (the acceptance criterion).** The orchestrator's `withBrokerDefaults` + `@ax/mcp-client` `filterByAgentScope` wildcard stays `allowedTools=[] && mcpConfigIds=[]`. The admin route's `rejectsWildcardScope` (‚â•1 tool or ‚â•1 MCP config) is UNCHANGED. An agent attached only to connectors still needs ‚â•1 allowedTool (or the dev-mode empty-empty wildcard) ‚Äî identical to a skill-only agent today. | This is the EXACT precedent skill_attachments set: a separate column that does not gate the sentinel. NOT a product decision ‚Äî connectors mechanically don't belong in the host tool-dispatcher catalog binding (`mcpConfigIds` = `mcp.<configId>.<tool>` visibility via filterByAgentScope), whereas a connector's MCP servers reach the agent as sandbox `.mcp.json` installed-entries (foldConnectorCaps), an ORTHOGONAL mechanism gated by the SDK. TASK-98's overloading actually mis-fed connector ids into filterByAgentScope as host mcp config ids ‚Äî reverting is a correctness fix, not just a refactor. | (a) make connectors count toward the sentinel ‚Äî REJECTED, would re-overload the field the card removes + diverge from skill_attachments. (b) block on "how does a connector-wildcard map" as a product decision ‚Äî REJECTED, the scoping-caution trigger does not fire: connectors never legitimately mapped to the wildcard sentinel (the sentinel is MCP+tools dev-bypass); skill_attachments already answered "an attachment-only agent isn't a wildcard". |
| 2026-06-01 | **The orchestrator union reads attachments as a THIRD source inside `resolveEffectiveConnectors`, resolving each attached id via `connectors:resolve` (owner-scoped, deduped against defaults + owner's-own).** Pass `agent.connectorAttachments` into `resolveEffectiveConnectors(bus, ctx, attachments)`. | The resolved `agent` already flows into runAgentInvoke (line 1204); `connectors:resolve` is owner-scoped (store `getByIdNotDeleted(userId, connectorId)`), so an attached connector resolves under the agent owner = the chat user (personal agents). Folds through the EXISTING `foldConnectorCaps` (no second materialization path, invariant #4). NON-FATAL per the existing union posture (a resolve miss skips that connector, never widens reach). | (a) a 4th separate fold path for attachments ‚Äî REJECTED, duplicates foldConnectorCaps (I4). (b) resolve attachments in @ax/agents and return folded caps from agents:resolve ‚Äî REJECTED, the orchestrator is the materialization owner + would couple @ax/agents to connector caps. |
| 2026-06-01 | **AgentForm writes connector ids to the new store via a dedicated `PATCH /admin/agents/:id/connector-attachments` (mirroring skill-attachments), NOT via agents:create/update's `mcpConfigIds`.** For a NEW agent the connector section saves after first create (same deferral skill_attachments uses ‚Äî "New agents get their section after first save"). The connector picker's selections no longer feed the create/update body's mcpConfigIds (reverted to []). Idempotent migration: existing agents whose connector ids were stuffed into `mcpConfigIds` are NOT auto-migrated at the data layer (ax-next has no prod data; mcpConfigIds genuinely held MCP config ids historically too, so a blind migration would misclassify real MCP ids as connectors). The migration is idempotent-by-construction (the new column defaults to []); existing connectors keep folding while attached via the new picker. | The card says "existing attachments migrated if needed; idempotent migration". With no prod data + the field's dual historical meaning (MCP ids AND TASK-98 connector ids are indistinguishable), a data migration that reclassifies mcpConfigIds‚ÜíconnectorAttachments would corrupt genuine MCP bindings. The honest idempotent migration is the additive NOT-NULL-DEFAULT-'[]' column (every existing row reads [] safely) + the UI moving the write to the new store. No regression: a connector attached via the new picker folds via the union (TASK-97 path). | (a) auto-copy every agent's mcpConfigIds into connector_attachments on migrate ‚Äî REJECTED, can't distinguish a real MCP config id from a TASK-98 connector id ‚Üí would mis-bind. (b) a backfill keyed on "id exists in connectors table" ‚Äî REJECTED, over-engineering for zero prod rows + still racy vs MCP ids that happen to match a connector id. |

## 2026-06-01 ‚Äî Fold credentials into connectors (remove Credentials tab)

Design: `docs/plans/2026-06-01-credentials-into-connectors-design.md` (source of truth, approved in brainstorm).

| Date | Decision | Rationale | Alternatives |
|---|---|---|---|
| 2026-06-01 | **Service-tag derivation lives in FOUR places, not the two the design names.** Design lists `connectors/src/credential-plan.ts` + `channel-web/src/lib/connectors.ts`. Reality also has `chat-orchestrator/src/connector-union.ts` + `connector-card.ts` (and `skill-broker/request-capability.ts`) re-deriving `slot.account ?? connectorId`. **Resolution: change only the two named `serviceTagForSlot` fns + drop `account` from the connectors `CapabilitySlotSchema`.** The connectors store re-validates capabilities on read (`store.ts` `validateCapabilities`), so dropping `account` from the connector schema STRIPS it on every read ‚Üí the orchestrator/skill-broker (which resolve via store-parsed hooks) see `account===undefined` and their `?? connectorId` fallback collapses to connectorId automatically. Runtime stays consistent (invariant #4) with zero orchestrator edits. | The orchestrator's `account` is a GENERAL skills+connectors capability mechanism (`skills-parser/capabilities.ts:10`, `orchestrator.ts` foldAuthoredSkillCaps uses `account:<svc>` for skill slots too). Removing it there would break skills + expand scope into another plugin's tests for inputs the connector store can no longer produce. | (a) Also edit orchestrator/connector-card/skill-broker ‚Üí rejected: out of design scope, touches skill-cap path, breaks orchestrator tests that feed `account` directly (testing an input now impossible for connectors). Tracked as optional follow-up: vestigial `slot.account` reads in connector-union/connector-card are now dead-but-harmless. |
| 2026-06-01 | **`CredentialSlotForm` has NO Remove button today** ‚Äî `onCleared` is a prop on the form + `CredentialSlotRow` but the form never renders Remove or calls it; Remove lived only in `KeysTab` (being deleted). Design change #3 assumes "Replace/Remove via the form's existing onCleared." **Resolution: wire the dead `onCleared` ‚Äî add a Remove button to `CredentialSlotForm` shown only when `current.set`, calling `clearDestinationCredential` + `onCleared`.** | The design names the form's onCleared as the mechanism; it's the one-source-of-truth (invariant #4) home for Remove. Form tests use `set:false` so no Remove renders there ‚Üí unaffected. | (a) Implement Remove only in the Connect dialog wrapper ‚Üí rejected: duplicates clear logic, contradicts "via the form's onCleared". Side effect: ProvidersPanel + RoutinesList sheets gain a Remove for set keys (benign improvement; verify their tests). |
| 2026-06-01 | **Implement directly (not subagent-per-task).** | The change is tightly coupled ‚Äî two `serviceTagForSlot` mirrors must stay byte-identical, shared presence logic, and the schema strip ripples through ~5 backend test files. A subagent split risks the two derivations diverging. Context budget healthy. | Subagent-driven-development per yolo-ship default (rejected for this coupling). |
| 2026-06-01 | **`serviceTagForSlot` keeps its `(slot, connectorId)` two-arg signature; body returns `connectorId`; slot param renamed `_slot`** (lint `^_` ignore). | Minimizes call-site churn (deriveCredentialPlan unchanged) and lets the test prove "legacy account tag ignored" by passing a slot WITH account and asserting connectorId. | Single-arg `serviceTagForSlot(connectorId)` (rejected ‚Äî loses the direct ignore-account assertion; more churn). |
| 2026-06-01 | **`connectors:delete` purge: `credentials:delete` declared as `optionalCalls` + `bus.hasService` guard; failures logged + swallowed.** Mirrors `@ax/routines` sync.ts posture. Connector loaded BEFORE softDelete (getByIdNotDeleted returns null after). ownerId = userId (user scope) / null (global). | A stripped preset without `@ax/credentials` must still delete the connector (degraded: key lingers). A credential hiccup must never wedge connector deletion. No new hook signature (credentials:delete already exists). | Hard `calls` dep (rejected ‚Äî breaks credential-less presets). |

### 2026-06-01 ‚Äî ax-code-reviewer findings (whole-branch review before PR)

| Date | Decision | Rationale | Alternatives |
|---|---|---|---|
| 2026-06-01 | **BLOCKER fix: reject `keyMode:'workspace'` on the user authoring route** (`rejectAdminOnlyFields`, connectors/admin-routes.ts). Reviewer found a non-admin could create-then-delete a `workspace`-keyMode connector (allowed by the user route ‚Äî it only gated `visibility`/`defaultAttached`) and the new purge-on-delete would tombstone the SHARED global key `account:<id>` (owner-independent) ‚Üí cross-tenant credential DoS. | The global credential WRITE is already admin-gated (/admin/destinations); the connector that drives the global PURGE must be too. With workspace rejected on the user route, non-admins own only private/personal connectors ‚Üí their purge only ever hits their OWN (scope:user, ownerId:userId) rows. Fixes at the same authz layer where visibility/defaultAttached are gated. | (a) skip global purge in the hook ‚Üí rejected: breaks the legit admin purge-on-delete; the hook can't see admin-ness. Bug-Fix-Policy regression tests added (user create + PATCH-flip to workspace ‚Üí 400). |
| 2026-06-01 | **SHOULD-FIX: widen the account-service destination regex** (`/^[a-z][a-z0-9-]{0,63}$/` ‚Üí `/^[a-z0-9][a-z0-9_-]{0,127}$/`) in @ax/credentials-admin-routes/destination-routes.ts. | Service is now ALWAYS the connector id (id grammar allows leading digit + `_`, e.g. `1password`, `my_crm`); the stricter destination grammar 400'd those, making such connectors unconnectable once the `account`-tag workaround was removed. Loosening-only; still excludes `:`. Test added (round-trip `1password_cli`). | Tighten connectorId grammar (rejected ‚Äî breaks existing stored ids). |
| 2026-06-01 | **SHOULD-FIX: retarget stale `slot.account ?? id` comments** in connector-union.ts / connector-card.ts / skill-broker request-capability.ts to say the `?? connectorId` is VESTIGIAL for connectors (store strips `account` on read) and only live for skill slots. Code unchanged (runtime-safe). | Invariant-#4 honesty ‚Äî the comments asserted a connector behavior that no longer happens. | Remove the dead reads (rejected ‚Äî the shape is shared with skill caps; orchestrator.ts:2753 is the general capability-card builder where `account` IS live for skills, left untouched). |

### 2026-06-01 ‚Äî ax-code-reviewer round 2 (BLOCKER only partially fixed)

| Date | Decision | Rationale | Alternatives |
|---|---|---|---|
| 2026-06-01 | **BLOCKER (round 2): gate the GLOBAL credential purge at the delete PRIMITIVE, not just the HTTP route.** Round-1's `rejectAdminOnlyFields` keyMode gate only covered `/settings/connectors`; the authored-connector approve path (`connector_propose` tool ‚Üí `connectors:install-authored` ‚Üí non-admin approval ‚Üí `applyAuthoredConnectorGrant` promotes via the `connectors:upsert` HOOK with `keyMode: draft.keyMode`) is a 2nd non-admin door to owning a live workspace connector ‚Üí delete ‚Üí global-key DoS. Fix: `connectors:delete` gains `purgeGlobal?: boolean` (default false); `deleteConnector` skips `scope:'global'` entries unless set; both route destroy handlers pass `purgeGlobal: actor.isAdmin`. Closes ALL paths (route, authored, legacy) at the operation. Tests: hook purgeGlobal:false‚Üíno global purge (the security regression) + purgeGlobal:true‚Üípurged; route test admin-destroy purges / non-admin-destroy doesn't. Kept the round-1 route keyMode gate as defense-in-depth. | Reviewer's Option A (skip global purge entirely) ‚Äî **rejected**: it would orphan a workspace connector's global company key on delete with NO UI home (this PR removes the Credentials tab; the AI-model-keys tab is provider-keys-only), violating the design's core "no secret lingers" goal. Option C (authority flag) is secure AND preserves admin purge-on-delete. The reviewer's "the hook can't distinguish authorized from unauthorized" is resolved by passing the caller-granted authority (`purgeGlobal`), an invariant-#5-minimized flag. | (a) skip global entirely (orphans the key); (b) gate keyMode at every write chokepoint incl. the promote path (more surface, doesn't fix legacy-owned state). |
| 2026-06-01 | **CORRECTION to the round-1 decision:** my claim that `orchestrator.ts:2753` is "the general capability-card builder where account is live for skills" was WRONG. The reviewer showed it's inside `applyAuthoredConnectorGrant` (the CONNECTOR grant path); `draft.proposal` is store-stripped of `account`, so the read is vestigial-for-connectors exactly like the other 3 sites. Retargeted that comment too. | Factual error caught by the reviewer ‚Äî `applyAuthoredCapabilityGrant` (skill twin) has no account row-builder; the live skill account path is `foldAuthoredSkillCaps`. | ‚Äî |

## 2026-06-02 ‚Äî Agents tab ‚Üí user Settings; non-admins manage their own agents

| Date | Decision | Rationale | Alternatives |
|---|---|---|---|
| 2026-06-02 | **Move "Agents" from the Admin nav to the user "Settings" nav** (AdminSidebar USER_NAV + AdminShell TAB_META eyebrow Settings); visible to every user. | User: even non-admins should list+manage their own agents. Agent CRUD (`/admin/agents` create/list/show/update/destroy) is ALREADY `requireUser` + owner-scoped ‚Äî only the nav hid it. | ‚Äî |
| 2026-06-02 | **Open the admin-only attachment routes to non-admin OWNERS, owner-scoped** (`/admin/agents/:id/{skill,connector}-attachments`): replace `if (!isAdmin) 403` with a workspace-connector guard. The attachment HOOKS already enforce owner-or-admin (`assertWriteAllowed`); the route gate was the only block. Security rule: a non-admin's set is rejected iff any **directly-attached OR skill-referenced** connector resolves owner-scoped (`connectors:resolve {userId: actor.id}`) to **keyMode:'workspace'** ‚Äî the only path to a GLOBAL/company credential. Personal connectors (the user's own per-user key) are their own reach ‚Üí no escalation. Not-owned/dangling ids are runtime no-ops ‚Üí tolerated (matches existing orphan tolerance). Admin bypasses. Fail-closed if `connectors:resolve` is absent (reject non-admin attach of a non-empty connector set). | User chose "Full: attach own connectors/skills (owner-scoped); workspace/shared stay admin-only." | (a) keep admin-only (rejected ‚Äî user wants full); (b) basic CRUD only (rejected ‚Äî agents couldn't use picked connectors). |
| 2026-06-02 | **Add `connectors:resolve` as an `optionalCall` to @ax/agents** (the attachment routes call it to check keyMode). Boundary review: alternate impl = @ax/connectors-sqlite registers the same hook; payload `{userId,connectorId}`‚Üí`{keyMode,...}` storage-agnostic; one-way agents‚Üíconnectors (connectors never calls agents ‚Üí no cycle); not an IPC action. | Needed for the owner-scoped keyMode guard. | Embed the check in the orchestrator at runtime (rejected ‚Äî write-time validation is the right place + less invasive). |
| 2026-06-02 | **Keep `AuthoredSkillsSection` (the agent's model-proposed skill DRAFTS + approval) admin-only for now**; hide it for non-admins in AgentForm; `/admin/agents/:id/authored-skills*` routes stay admin-gated. | The user's ask is "attach connectors/skills" = SkillAttachmentsSection (attach existing skills) + the connector picker. Authored-skill approval is a distinct capability-grant flow deserving its own security pass. Tracked as a follow-up. | Open it now (rejected ‚Äî scope + separate security surface). |

| 2026-06-02 | **FIX (review Finding 1): `setSkillAttachments` must pass `ownerUserId: actor.id` to `skills:resolve`.** Without it, `skills:resolve` returns only GLOBAL catalog skills (plugin.ts:575) ‚Äî so a non-admin attaching their OWN user-scoped skill (the picker now lists `/settings/skills`) resolved to `[]` ‚Üí validator `skill-not-found` ‚Üí 400, silently breaking the feature. Passing ownerUserId unions global + the caller's user-scoped skills (user-wins); a superset for admins (no regression) and it also lets the workspace-connector guard see a user-scoped skill's referenced connectors (closes the over-stated-guarantee Finding 3). Test stub now models ownerUserId (user-scoped ids only when passed); the 200-path test uses a genuinely user-scoped skill so it would catch the regression. | Caught by the pre-PR ax-code-reviewer; the original test stub resolved ids regardless of ownerUserId, masking it. | ‚Äî |

Backfill (existing agents ‚Üí `.ax/`) is Phase 2. So prepending the full string in normal mode injects only the augment block in practice, and the acceptance criterion "augment still prepends on top of composed result" is satisfied. | Try to split the augment block back out of the string (rejected ‚Äî no delimiter survives the host-side merge; fragile). Pass augment as a separate runner field (rejected ‚Äî schema change, out of Phase 1 scope; the existing field already carries it). |

Matches v1's operating-manual-first ordering (AGENTS.md before identity) and keeps the safety floor first among runner-authored content so a long evolved SOUL.md can't push it out of the model's primacy window. | Design ¬ßrunner-prompt-engine specifies `[safety floor] + [AGENTS.md if present] + ## Identity + ## Soul + evolution guidance + operational notes`; v1 put the operating manual first; I follow that exactly. | 2026-06-02 | TASK-139 open-question 3 (budget policy) PINNED: NO renderMinimal/drop machinery in Phase 1 ‚Äî the modules are all small fixed runner prose EXCEPT the inject-if-present `.ax/` files, which are agent-authored and unbounded. Policy: inject each `.ax/` file in full; do not truncate or drop in Phase 1. If a file read exceeds a generous hard cap (256 KiB) the runner skips that single file with a logged warning (a runaway/corrupt file can't blow the prompt) ‚Äî it does not truncate mid-content. | v1's per-module token-budget allocator is over-engineered for Phase 1 (4 short fixed modules + 3 small identity files). Drop-when-tight is a real concern only once identity files grow large; that's a follow-up, not MVP. The 256 KiB per-file guard is the thin safety net (a corrupt multi-MB file is the only realistic blow-up), implemented as skip-with-warn not truncate so identity is never silently half-injected. | Port v1's allocateModules budget allocator (rejected ‚Äî YAGNI for Phase 1; 4 fixed modules don't need a priority/minimal allocator). Truncate large files mid-content (rejected ‚Äî silently corrupts identity; skip-whole-file-with-warning is honest). |

Phase 2's bootstrap route will import the BOOTSTRAP string from here (or it gets re-homed then if a second consumer appears). | New `@ax/agent-identity` package (rejected ‚Äî premature; one consumer at Phase 1, no cross-plugin-import need yet). Ship as `.md` files copied by postbuild (rejected ‚Äî adds a copy step + runtime fs read of a packaged asset vs. a compiled-in constant). |
